antu samuttīrṇapratijñāpāraṁ pārāvārapāravaneydidāgaḷ
gaṅgādvāradoḷ bandu kāṇba makuṭabaddharuṁ tadvēdītaṭadoḷ band’ eṟagu
vadhikārigaḷuṁ śibirabahirbhāgadoḷ bandu kaikoṇḍa sainyaṅgaḷuṁ berasu,

neredantaḥpurakānteyar palabaruṁ sēsikkeyuṁ vārasauṁ
dariyar cāmaramikkeyuṁ makuṭabaddhādhīśarāgaḷ vasuṁ
dhareyaṁ parvire maiyanikkeyumudāttōtsāhadiṁ rājamaṁ
diramaṁ pokkanudārasāravibhavaṁ saṁsārasārōdayaṁ // Ādi.12.129 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]


idu dēvēndramunīndravandyaparamajinēndramukhacandra-
vākcandrikāprasaraprasādōdīrṇasūktikallōlamālākīrṇa-
kavitāguṇārṇavapraṇītamappādipurāṇadoḷ
māgadhadarpadaḷanaṁ
dvādaśāśvāsaṁ

[p. 274]
[trayōdaśāśvāsaṁ]

śrīyoḷoḍambaḍisi jaya
śrīyaṁ ṣaṭkhaṇḍamaṇḍaḷakṣitiyumanā
tmīyaṁ māḍuven emba ni
jāyatiyindaṁ sarasvatīmaṇihāraṁ // Ādi.13.1 [kandaṁ]

antu bharatēśvaracakravarti dakṣiṇadigaṅganāḷaṅkāran āgi naḍedu
dakṣiṇāmburāśiyaneydi vaijayantīdvāradoḷ bīḍaṁ biṭṭāgaḷ,

ēlālavaṅgalavalī
vēlāvanabhūmiyoḷ nidhīśvarasainya
vyālagajaṅgaḷ vanagaja
līleyananukarisi kaṇgevanduvu palavuṁ // Ādi.13.2 [kandaṁ]

antā vanōpāntadoḷ munninante śibiramaṁ niṟisi vaijayantīdvāra-
doḷagaṇindamonde rathadoḷ lavaṇajaladhiyaṁ pokku,

māgadharaṁ geldantevo
lāgaḍe varatanuvanotti kappaṅgoṇḍu
dyōgada kalitanamaṁ poga
ḻvāgaḷavāṅmanasagōcaraṁ pauravanā // Ādi.13.3 [kandaṁ]

antu varatanuvina kaiyoḷabhēdyakavacamumaṁ cūḍāratnamumaṁ
ratnakaṭakaṁ berasu palavuṁ parārthyaratnaṅgaḷaṁ koṇḍu maguḻdu lavaṇasamudradupa-
samudrada naḍuve naḍedu candanapanasanāḷikēratāmbūlavallīpracurapradēśaṅgaḷoḷ
nijavijayakuñjaraṅgaḷaṁ vihārisi bandu sindhudvāradoḷ samudrakallōla-
līlāndōḷitavanadēvatāndōḷanānukāritāmbūlalatikālambakramukamumā-
kampitamadhukaranikarānukāri latāgr̥hapradīpacampakamuṁ praṅkhōḷitamanasija
[p. 275]
vijayapraśastilēkhanōcitacchadaśrītāḷikamum appa vēḷāvanadoḷāvāsitavijaya-
kaṭakan āgi pūrvasthitiyoḷe pōgi,

jaḷadhiya nīranadondāṁ
goḷagina nīrendu bagedu dāṇṭida vasudhā
taḷapatigittaṁ trāsaṁ
goḷutuṁ sarvasvamaṁ prabhāsāmaranuṁ // Ādi.13.4 [kandaṁ]

ant’ ā prabhāsāmaranaṁ nijavijayayaśaḥprabhāsamūhadindaṁ pudidu
sindhunadītīrambiḍidu barpalli,

eḷavisilīgaḷīgaḷe mudirdudu cūtakujātamīgaḷī
gaḷe nanedōṟitindoḷadinunmadaṣaṭpadavr̥ndamīgaḷī
gaḷe moredattu candanada taḷkabaḷānikarakkadīgaḷī
gaḷe negaḻdattelē pugiladāgale vēḍa vasantarājanā // Ādi.13.5 [campakamāle]

jinuguva tumbiyiñcarame gāṇara kākaḷi kūḍe sōrva mā
vina sone gandhasindhuramadaṁ taḷirōḷi taguḷdu taḷta kē
tanatati cāmarōtkaradelar maḷayāniḷanāge rājarā
jana paḍe celvanēneḻedukoṇḍudo banda basantarājanā // Ādi.13.6 [campakamāle]

mattam atyantadhautakaladhautasthāsakāḷaṅkr̥tanakṣatramāḷāparikalitakarīndraṅgaḷe
vikacakarṇikākāranikīrṇajaṅgamakrīḍāgirīndraṅgaḷāge, sakaladikpracaḷitarājaputra-
mayūrātapatranicayame sañcārībhūtacūtabhūjārāmamāge, vijaya-
kausumbharaktāṁśukapatākānikāyame pallavitāśōkavanamāge, madāmōda-
surabhiyuṁ madaśīkarāsāraśiśiramuṁ madāmōdabharamantharamuṁ appa
karikarṇatāḷāniḷane maḷayaruhanandanāndōḷanōdgandhiyuṁ maḷayagiri-
nirjharāsphāḷitaśītaḷamuṁ maḷayaviḷāsinīnirantarāḷastanataṭaskhalanamanda-
mandagamanamum appa maḷayāniḷan āge,

kariṇīvr̥ndavrajōdgāyanasamudayakarṇāmr̥tasyandihindō
ḷaravaṁ sāmōdanānāvidhakusumarasāpānasānandabhr̥ṅgau
gharavaṁ tāvāge puṣpōtkarabaḷavijayōddarpakandarpalīlā
karanādaṁ jaitrayātrōtsavadoḷakhiḷaṣaṭkhaṇḍabhūmaṇḍalēśaṁ // Ādi.13.7 [mahāsragdhare]

antu digvijayayātreye vasantōdyānayātreyananukarise,


[p. 276]
salilakrīḍābhavōdyajjaḷakaṇanikarākāramattadvipēndrā
vaḷihastāgrōccaḷacchīkarasamudayamudyānakēḷīcaḷatpa
triḷaśākhākārajaitradviradakadaḷikāḍambaraṁ bhūrikōḷā
haḷasēnācakravāḷaṁ naḍedudu vijayaśrīvadhūtkaṇṭheyindaṁ // Ādi.13.8 [mahāsragdhare]

ant’ atyantapravardhamānavijayōdyōgadiṁ vijayārdhācaḷō-
pāntamanoyyanoyyaneydivarpāgaḷ,

ciravikṣōbhitasindhutōyaśiśiraṁ tattīranānālatō
tkarasaṅghaṭṭanamantharaṁ madapayaḥkaṇḍūḷagaṇḍasthaḷa
dviradōdghr̥ṣṭaghanasravatsaraḷasārāmōdamuddāmabhr̥ṁ
garavaṁ cakriyānāṟisittu vijayārdhōpāntamandāniḷaṁ // Ādi.13.9 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

mattam ant’ante barevare,

gaganābhōgamaneyde nīḷda maṇikūṭāṭōpamembente di
ṭṭige munnaṁ bare sāre sāre tanuvaṁ tatkuñjasañjātabhū
jagaḷatpuṣpaparāgasaurabhavahanmandānilaṁ sōṅke to
ṭṭage kaṇgoṇḍudu pauravaṅge vijayārdhādrīndraśōbhōdayaṁ // Ādi.13.10 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

ā vijayārdhada kaḍeviḍidu mēge negeda vanavēdikāpradēśa-
maneydidāgaḷ,

adaṟoḷage pudida sapta
cchadacampakanāgapūgapunnāgavanaṁ
pudida posagampinoḷ baḷa
sidudāgaḷ puguva bharatanantaḥpuramaṁ // Ādi.13.11 [kandaṁ]

antu sogayisuva vanavēdikeya nānāmaṇimayūkhamālāvirāji-
tōttuṅgatōraṇadvāradindaṁ nuguḷdu vanavīthiviḍidu bandu vijayārdha-
madhyamakūṭāsannapradēśanivēśitaśibiran āgi niyamadoḷirda bharatēśvara-
cakravartiyiravanaṟidu,

sitakusumaśēkharaṁ ca
rcitacandananativiḷāsavidhr̥tadukūlaṁ

[p. 277]
dhr̥taratnārghyaṁ bandaṁ
patigidiraṁ śaṅkhanidhiye barpantāgaḷ // Ādi.13.12 [kandaṁ]

maṇimakuṭaṁ śikharaṁ laṁ
baṇigeya posamuttu nirjharaṁ maṇikaṭakaṁ
maṇikaṭakamāge tadgiri
geṇeyādaṁ tanna pesaroḷaṁ vijayārdhaṁ // Ādi.13.13 [kandaṁ]

bandu maṇimakuṭanasavasa
dindaṁ cakriya podaḻda tējakke masu
ḷdandeṟagi munde nilvudu
mondavayavadinde sāre karedu nr̥pēndraṁ // Ādi.13.14 [kandaṁ]

bhadrāsanamanikkavēḻe kuḷḷirdu vijayārdhakumāraṁ

idu vijayārdhamenna pesaruṁ vijayārdhamalaṅghyamendumiṁ
tidu peṟargānuminnegamalaṅghyaneniṁ ninagāḷenāḷa le
kkadoḷidu cakravartigaḷa digvijayārdhadoḷondi ninduda
ppudaṟoḷe sandudī giriyumī jagadoḷ vijayārdhanāmadiṁ // Ādi.13.15 [campakamāle]

idaṟoḷ madhyamakūṭadoḷ vasiyipeṁ ninnājñe pūmāleyaṁ
dade nindirpudu matkirīṭataṭadoḷ cakrēśarār bandoḍaṁ
modaloḷ māḻpa niyōgamintidenagendānandadiṁ tāne mā
ḍidanā cakrige nāḍeyuṁ vibhavadiṁ puṇyōdakasnānamaṁ // Ādi.13.16 [campakamāle]

antu vijayābhiṣēkaṅgeydu,

sāramidu ratnamayabhr̥ṁ
gāraṁ haripīṭhamidu jagattritayāḷaṁ
kāramidu divyamātapa
vāraṇamamr̥tāṁśubimbadhavaḷaviḷāsaṁ // Ādi.13.17 [kandaṁ]

ivu camarījātaṁ du
gdhavārdhiphēnōpamānamivu ninageye ta
kkuvu ninna jasada rūpino
ḷive meṟevuvu sakaḷacakravartiśrīyaṁ // Ādi.13.18 [kandaṁ]


[p. 278]
endu vijayārdhakumāraṁ sāravastugaḷanōlagisi tanagājñāvidhēyan āgi
pōdaṁ. annegaṁ bharatēśvaracakravartiyumalli cakraratnamaṁ pūjisi,

vijayārdhajayamidenagā
va jayaṁ negaḻduttarārdhajayame jayaṁ di
gvijayadoḷendūrjitabhuja
vijayaṁ digvijayacinteyiṁ toḍardāgaḷ // Ādi.13.19 [kandaṁ]

antu tanna munne banda vanavīthiyoḷagane maguḻdu pōgi vēdikādvāradiṁ
poṟamaṭṭu vijayārdhavanavēdikāsannaviśālapradēśadoḷ,

nelevīḍaṁ bīḍumāḍal kelavudivasamaṁ māḻpudinnilli rūpyā
calamaṁ pāyduttarārdhakkemage naḍeva sāmagriyaṁ māḍalīgaḷ
nele gaṅgāsindhumadhyakṣitipatigaḷumī tāṇadoḷ bandu kāṇbar
palarendantalli celvāgire biḍisidanur‍vīśvaraṁ tanna bīḍaṁ // Ādi.13.20 [mahāsragdhare]

antu bīḍaṁ biṭṭirpannegaṁ gaṅgāsindhugaḷeraḍaṟeḍeya bhūpāḷarinde
munna vr̥ṣabhanāthana naḍapidudumaṁ tamma naṇpumaṁ bagedu kururājādi-
mūrdhābhiṣiktapārthivar sannaddhabalaparivr̥tar āgi bharatēśvaracakravartiya-
nāsthānadoḷ bandu kaṇḍu,

oḍevude vajrakavāṭama
naḍarvude vijayārdhagiriyanintīgaḷe pū
[ḻde]ḍegi[ḍipu]de sindhuvaniṁ
taḍevandamidāvudemmanemmane besasā // Ādi.13.21 [kandaṁ]

ninaguttarārdhamonda
rdhanimēṣamuhūrtamātradiṁ bārade kai
ginituvaraṁ dēvar naḍe
vanituṁ māṇbanitumantadāvudu gahanaṁ // Ādi.13.22 [kandaṁ]

embannegamambaradoḷa
ḷumbaṁ beḷagenisi makuṭamaṇikuṇḍaladi
vyāmbarabhūṣitanamaraka
dambakavr̥tanorvanamaranā girivaradiṁ // Ādi.13.23 [kandaṁ]


[p. 279]
avatarisi cakriyaṁ kaṁ
ḍavanatamaṇimakuṭanucitapīṭhaniviṣṭaṁ
bhuvanēśaṁ besagoḷe vina
yavacaḥprasaraṅgaḷesedoḍambaḍe nuḍidaṁ // Ādi.13.24 [kandaṁ]

bhuvanakke kuśalamaṁ mā
ḍuva ninagēnendu kuśalamē embeṁ pēḻ
bhuvananuta māṇadarinr̥pa
bhuvanakkavvaḷipa tōḷge kuśalame ninnā // Ādi.13.25 [kandaṁ]

dēvara kuladoḷ puṭṭiye
dēvavesar negaḻdudemagakāraṇamadanā
mēvemo vijigīṣuteyiṁ
dēvanenal dēva nīve dēvane altē // Ādi.13.26 [kandaṁ]

idu nr̥patējaścakrada
podaḷke tānalte cakrarūpadinirda
ppudu ninna daṇḍanītiya
puduve valaṁ daṇḍaratnamembudu peṟatē // Ādi.13.27 [kandaṁ]

bhavadīyabaḷavijr̥mbhita
ravadiṁ trastanenadhīśa bandeṁ kāṇal
bhavadaṅghrisarōjamanā
navadhūtārātinr̥pa bhavatkiṅkaraneṁ // Ādi.13.28 [kandaṁ]

kr̥tamāḷanenembeniḷā
pratītaneṁ giritaṭaṅgaḷennaṟiyaduvi
lla tamisraguhākūṭa
sthitaneṁ nīnennanāḷvudāḷvesageyveṁ // Ādi.13.29 [kandaṁ]

endu tannaṁ munnamaṟipi,

beleyiḍalaṟivoḍe maṇḍali
beleyiḍugema nōḻpoḍivaṟa tējada mēlu
jjvalatēja ninna tējaṁ
nelasidud ene pēḻivarke belegaḷumoḷavē // Ādi.13.30 [kandaṁ]


[p. 280]
ondondaṟinī tuḍugega
ḷondondaggaḷamivendu padinālkumanō
rondane tōṟi nijādara
dindaṁ bharatēśvaraṅge divijaṁ koṭṭaṁ // Ādi.13.31 [kandaṁ]

antu koṭṭu tānuṁ cakravartiya mannaṇeyoḷ santasambaṭṭu
vijayārdhaguhādvārapravēśōpāyamanellamaṟiye binnapaṅgeydā vyantarāmaraṁ
pōgaloḍaṁ manuvaṁśadhvajaṁ sēnānāyakaṅge baḻiyanaṭṭidāgaḷātaṁ bandu munname
bandirda kururājādi pārthivaraṁ nōḍi,

avanīśādēśamaṁ dāṇṭidarenipa jagadduryaśōdhūḷiyuṁ pā
rthivasēnādhūḷiyuṁ muṭṭadu dalivaranembante mundiṭṭu bandi
rpavarudghakṣattrakaṇṭhīravarivaradhipar caṇḍadōrdaṇḍajaitrō
tsavasaudhōdagrakīrtidhvajarivare patiśrīlatōdyānapāḷar // Ādi.13.32 [mahāsragdhare]

embuduṁ taduktisudhāsāravāridhāreyindaṁ konarta rājaputrara
mārgaśramātapākrāntam appa manam emba lateyananēkakuśalālāpapraśneyindaṁ
kusumitamumaṁ svahastatāmbūladānadindaṁ phalitamumaṁ māḍi tamma tamma
bīḍugaḷgavaraṁ pōgalvēḻdu sēnānāyakana mogamaṁ nōḍi kr̥tamāḷāma-
rōddiṣṭōpāyamanellamaṁ pēḻdu,

teṟeva teṟanintuṭintī
teṟadinde tamisraguheya vajrada paḍiyaṁ
teṟedadaṟa beṅke pōpina
meṟagisu nīṁ mlēcchakhaṇḍamaṁ paḍuvaṇadaṁ // Ādi.13.33 [kandaṁ]

ene rathinīpati cakrē
śana besanaṁ pūṇdu rāgadindēṟi jaga
dvinutāśvaratnamaṁ piri
du naccinoḷ piḍidu daṇḍaratnamanāgaḷ // Ādi.13.34 [kandaṁ]

katipayaturaṅgabalapari
vr̥tanoḷapokkogeda sindhuvanavēdikeyiṁ
satatagativēgadindū
rjitabhujabaḷaneydi nagada vanavēdikeyaṁ // Ādi.13.35 [kandaṁ]


[p. 281]
ā vēdikeya mūḍaṇa maṇimayasōpānaṅgaḷindaṁ rajatācaḷa-
jagatītaḷamanēṟi tannoḍaneya balamellamaṁ paḍuvaṇa sōpānaṅgaḷindaṁ beṅke
bhōṅkenaḷuradantu bēgaṁ mlēcchakhaṇḍāntarvartiyāge munnaṁ kaḻipi
guhōtsaṅgamaṁ tānorbaneydevandu turagaratnamanēṟi paścimābhimukhan āgi nindu
bharatēśvaracakravarti gelgendu sātirēkaṁ dvādaśayōjanavistārāṣṭayōjanōtsēdha-
vajrakavāṭapuṭaṅgaḷaṁ,

bharadindaṁ daṇḍadoḷ tāṭisidoḍe vijayārdhācaḷaṁ toṭṭanāgaḷ
biridattembantumā parvatamaḷaṟidudembantumākāśamāśāṁ
taradindaṁ pattuviṭṭī dharege keḍedudembantumāśaṅke poṇmu
ttire percittugraghōṣaṁ praḷayaghanaghaṭāṭōpagambhīraghōṣaṁ // Ādi.13.36 [mahāsragdhare]

ararīpuṭameraḍuṁ jī
rgaredu maraldandamentuṭāytenna bhayaṁ
karadaṇḍaratnahatiyiṁ
giri nondu naraḷva māḻkeyantāytāgaḷ // Ādi.13.37 [kandaṁ]

teṟeyaloḍamalli beṅkeya
poṟamaḍuvondandamanitu kāladoḷenduṁ
poṟamaḍade bhōṅkenāgaḷ
poṟamaṭṭavolāduduṣṇadīrghōcchvāsaṁ // Ādi.13.38 [kandaṁ]

ant’ abhēdyavajrakavāṭapuṭaṅgaḷā parvataderdedeṟevante teṟeye
bhōṅkenaḷurva beṅkeyaṁ sōṅkalīyade,

koseyaninisaṟipi kuḍe laṁ
ghisidudu panneraḍuyōjanambaraminnē
vesagoḷvudo kaḍuvēgadi
nasakaḻidudu manamumaṁ turaṅgamaratnaṁ // Ādi.13.39 [kandaṁ]

antu turaṅgaratnada javadoḷoḍambaṭṭante sakaḷacamūpatiyu
manaśvaratnamumaṁ daṇḍaratnamumaṁ meymeyyoḷe kāva dēvategaḷ vijayārdhataṭa-
vēdikeyiṁ taguḷdu sindhuvina paścimadigbhāgavanavēdikeya tōraṇadvāradindaṁ
mlēcchakhaṇḍadoḷagaṇa vividhākārapuragrāmasīmābhirāmabhūmibhāgamaṁ
pugisidāgaḷ sēnānāyakaṁ mlēcchakhaṇḍamaṁ pradakṣiṇaṅgeydu bāykēḷisi palambar
[p. 282]
mlēccharājaranavaravara jīvadhana kuladhanaṅgaḷ verasu mundiṭṭu tōraṇadvāradindaṁ
sindhuvanavēdikeyoḷagane bandu sōpānāntaradoḷī vijayārdhataṭavēdikeyaṁ
kaḻidu jagatītaḷamanēṟi barpannegaṁ,

oḷagaṇa beṅkeyanaṟudiṁ
gaḷantu nagamuguḻdu śāntarūpadinirda
ttaḷuruttamirda kōpā
naḷanindupaśāntanāda bhūbhr̥tpativōl // Ādi.13.40 [kandaṁ]

āgaḷ ā guhādvāramaṁ patākinīpati paḍege naḍeyalimbappantu śōdhisi
kāpaṁ pēḻdu nijavijayaśibiramaṁ pokku cakravallabhanāsthānamaṇṭapadoḷ
dūrāvanatamaṇimakuṭan āgi kaṇḍu vastuvāhanapurassaraṁ mlēccharājaraṁ lalāṭaspr̥ṣṭa-
bhūtaḷaraṁ māḍi kāṇisi,

harikarikanyāratnā
bharaṇaṅgaḷ dēva kuladhanādigaḷivu dē
varadondājñeyanāmpar
kirīṭadindivargaḷinibaruṁ bhūpatigaḷ // Ādi.13.41 [kandaṁ]

end’ avara dēśanāmakulagōtraṅgaḷaṁ neṟeye tiḷiye binnapaṅgeydu
bhr̥tyabhāvamaṁ pūṇisi sanmānadānaṅgaḷoḷ santasambaḍisi tantamma nelegaḷge
pōgalvēḻdu śubhadinamuhūrtadoḷ uttarabharatavijayōdyōgamaṁ
bharatarājanaṟipalendu vijayabhēriyaṁ poyisidāgaḷ,

desegaḷa sandaṁ paṟidā
gasadindaṁ pattuviḍisuvantevoliḷeyaṁ
masakadoḷe pottu negevavo
lesedudu digvijayabhūribhērīninadaṁ // Ādi.13.42 [kandaṁ]

ā vijayaprayāṇabhērīninādamambhōbhāragambhīrāmbhōdharastanita-
bahuḷasnigdhaṅgaḷ appa madastambēramabr̥ṁhitaṅgaḷindamasakr̥dāsphālitānēkadundubhi-
dhvanimadhuragambhīraṅgaḷ appa hayahēṣitaṅgaḷindamudagrakuñjarakumbhajarjaraṇa-
janitōtkaṇṭhakaṇṭhīravaravōdbhaṭabhairavaṅgaḷ appa subhaṭapaṭukṣvēḍitaṅgaḷindaṁ sandaṇisi
ghūrṇamānārṇavaghōṣamaṁ gelda harṣadiṁ percuvante perci,


[p. 283]
vīraśrīsnānakumbhadvayamenipa kaṭadvandadiṁ dānadhārā
sāraṁ kaigaṇme kaṇgoppuva jayagajamaṁ līleyindēṟi vādi
trārāvaṁ vandivr̥ndadhvanijayajayakōḷāhaḷaṁ maṅgaḷāḷaṁ
kāraṁ yātrōtsavaprastutam ene taḷardaṁ rāgadiṁ rājarājaṁ // Ādi.13.43 [sragdhare]

antu taḷardu rājamandiramaṁ poṟamaḍuvāgaḷ,

jaḷadhidvīpāntarāḷaṅgaḷanirade pugiṁ pōgimugrārigaḷ mā
rkoḷalāṟir cakranāthaprabaḷabaḷamanembantevol sānukūlā
niḷanindaṁ kētuhastāvaḷi miḷirvinegaṁ banduvuttuṅgabhūbhr̥
tkuḷasaṅkāśaṅgaḷākāśada neladeḍeyaṁ parve gandhadvipaṅgaḷ // Ādi.13.44 [mahāsragdhare]

antu poṟamaṭṭuttarabharatada vijayaśrīvivāhamahōtsavaprārambhadoḷ
dikpālakara kedaṟuva piṣṭātakacūrṇamenisuva rajaḥpuñjamumaṁ dikkanyakeyara sūsuva
lājāñjaḷinicayamenisuva madakarikaraśīkaranikaramumaṁ ambaradoḷamara-
vr̥ndaṅgaḷ bittarisuva patākegaḷenisuva karikadaḷikegaḷumaṁ munde mundaniladēvana
taḷiva kusumaprasaramenisuva turaṅgamukhaphēnapallavastabakamumaṁ nōḍuttuṁ
naḍeye,

baḷavatpratyantabhūpāḷakanikaramahāvāhinīvāhinīsaṁ
kuḷamatyutsāhadindaṁ puge desedeseyaṁ bandu cakrēśabhūbhr̥
tkuḷacakrāvārapāraṁ subhaṭajanacamatkāri tējōmahaurvā
naḷamugrārātivargapraḷayakaramadondeyde tāḷdittagurvaṁ // Ādi.13.45 [mahāsragdhare]

āgaḷ sainyādhināthanadhināthana keladoḷ pakṣagajādhirūḍhan āgi dēva-
nōḍī tōrpudu davadahanadhūmādhikaśyāmaḷitōttāḷatāḷakāyamati-
vicitratrapumayapatrakhacitōccaṇḍatāḷacāpadaṇḍamanēkavarṇākīrṇatrisaravēṇikāgāḍha-
grathitatrapuṣakōśaguptagulphāntaraprāptakhaḍgadhēnukamāndhradhānuṣkabaḷaṁ;

mattitta kōmaḷaśyāmaḷacchāyānikāyamuṁ upaniṭilaghaṭitakuṭilajūṭa-
bandhamumākūrpararacita kāḷāyasavaḷayabhayaṅkarakaradvayamumabhinava-

kaṁ[cu]kamatisubhaṭamadōtkaṭamidu karṇāṭabalaṁ;


[p. 284]
matt’ ī bhāgadoḷ abhinavapriyaṅguśyāmāṅgamardhacandrabudbuda-
vyākīrṇatriśūlakarāḷaviśālavētrakhēṭakamudghr̥ṣṭaraśmipāṇḍurapāḷita-
karavāḷāḍḍāyudhamikṣudaṇḍapraṇīta krīḍāvakhaṇḍitōccaṇḍaśuṇḍāḷagātrāparapati-
bāḷakadaḷikākāṇḍalīlācchinna sindhuramadhyahastamatyantamr̥dumr̥ṇāḷadaṇḍahēḷādaḷita-
dantidaśanamusaḷamutkavāṭalāghavalaṅghitaparapuraparikhāvaḷayamanēkāhavadr̥ṣṭa-
dōssāhasamidu varāṭasubhaṭabalaṁ;

matt’ itta sarvāṅgīṇasāndraharidravilēpanavilipta haritāḷapaṅkapiṅgaḷavilaṅghita-
śilāstambhavibhramaramānitambaśikharitaraṅgitacaturaṅguḷāgrapallavanivasanamatima-
sr̥ṇavarṇavyatikarōdīrṇaśōbhāpuñjarañjita nūpurapaṭṭikānaddhakanakapatrāṅkitā-
yōgakhaḍgaputrikōdbhāsamānasuvarṇakōśamanatijaraṭhakarṇikāramukuḷa-
sthūḷatricatura suvarṇamaṇibaddhōddhurakandhara mutkaṭahāṭaka padakamaṇi trikhaṇḍa-
karṇābharaṇamudbaddhōdbhavamatyantaśauryasaundar‍ya prakāśana parityaktatanucchadamuttaptaraja-
tāvadātalōhaputrikānaddhalākṣāhiṅgulikapāṭalaphalakamardhakaravāḷacāḷanaprakaṭita-
bhaṭabibhīṣikāḍambaramatisphuṭavīraśr̥ṅgāranāṭakābhinayanaṭavr̥ndamidu mahā-
nāṭakabalaṁ;

matt’ ittakārtasvarastambhasañcāraṇabhāsvaramāskandhapralambasubhaṭakarṇābharaṇa-
karṇapāśamābhīḷaśārdūlamukharōmakarāḷasr̥kvōpāntaprarūḍhaśmaśru-
jāḷamāhava mahāhuṅkārakāḷakūṭaviṭapiprarōhaśaṅkāvaha nābhikūpāvalambi-
kūrcakaḷāpaṁ lalāṭanihitakausumbhāṁśukapaṭṭakāprāntanibiḍanibaddhakēśabandha-
mācūḷasvastikabaddhavicitravastra dvayōddāmadhānuṣkamudvīcimarumarīcinicaya-
cañcaḷōddāmabaḷabahaḷaniṣkavacaprāsapāṇivārāśikamugrapuṅkhaprēkhōḷānēka-
nētrapaṭṭikāsaṭāḷasaraḷakuntahastamahāhayārōhaṇamasitabhujagaśiśutaraḷatara-
vārikhaḍgakhēṭakavyagrakaradvayōddāmapadātibahaḷamidu lāṭabalaṁ,

end’ anēka dēśādhīśabalaṅgaḷaṁ bēṟevēṟe tōṟuttuṁ barpannegaṁ munde,

ibhakhaḍgivrātanānāharimayakaṭakabhrājitaṁ tuṅgavaṁśa
prabhavaṁ siṁhāsanaśrīsamucitamamr̥tāmbhōdhikallōlamāḷā
nibhalīlāsañcaḷaccāmararuciramiḷācakravikhyātabhūbhr̥
tprabhu cakrādhīśanoḷ maccaripavolesedirdattu raupyācaḷēndraṁ // Ādi.13.46 [mahāsragdhare]


[p. 285]
antu vijayārdhācaḷakaṭakābhimukhīkr̥tanijavijayakaṭakan āgi

eraḍaṟoḷaṁ candrādi

[p. 286]
sindhuvinoḷ kūḍida guhāmadhyadoḷunmagnanimagnajalanimnagātaṭadoḷ bīḍaṁ
biḍisi,

ondaṟa nīr‍maḷalonda
rkondisutuṁ mēge koṇḍu negevudidēṁ ma

rdaḍige bare tegeva gāḷiyi
naḍigiḻidapudidaṟa nīridondaccariyē // Ādi.13.52 [kandaṁ]

endu binnapaṅgeydu divyaśaktiprabhāvadindamānuṣāraṇyaṅgaḷa mahādru-

daḷḷisi kukiluttambudhi

ttaḷḷāḍe nelaṁ balamadu

sakaṭōdghr̥ṣṭavanēbhatuṅgajaraṭhasthūḷārgaḷākāramā

ā guheyoḷagaṇa śaradado
ḷāgaḷe basavaḷida balamanāṟisuvavolā
ytā giriya koḷada maragaḷa
pūgaḷa kampane teraḷci bīsuva pavanaṁ // Ādi.13.56 [kandaṁ]

ant’ alli bīḍaṁ biṭṭu munnin ante paścimakhaṇḍamumaṁ akhaṇḍapratāpa-
dhvajanandu tanna dhvajinīpatiyanaṭṭi bāykēḷisi cakraratnamaṁ mundiṭṭu madhyamakhaṇḍa-
mumaṁ auṅki pūḻe pokkavaṣṭambhisi nindāgaḷ, [cilātā]vartarembirvaruṁ
mlēccharājar dhanurdharaprāyamuṁ aśvīyabahaḷamuṁ hāstikasādhanamum appa tamma

kaṇḍu mantrigaḷ mārkoṇḍu,

vijayārdhādriyanurci barpaḷavidēṁ sāmānyamē dēśamaṁ
bhujavikrāntadinotti pokka[da]ṭadēnāścaryamaltē mr̥ga
vrajadoḍḍēṁ mr̥garājanaṁ neṟevudē tāṅgalke nammī br̥ha
ddhvajinīsaṅkuḷamī jigīṣuvanidēṁ saṅgrāmadoḷ gelgumē // Ādi.13.57 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

ad’ alladeyuṁ ī giridurgamaṁ dāṇṭi banda ballāḷ divyaprabhāvanakkum a-
mōghanakkuṁ; adaṟiṁ ītanoḷ idirci kāduva maruḷtanaṁ bēḍa; himavadvi-
jayārdhagaṅgāsindhutaṭāvadhiyappī namma madhyamakhaṇḍadoḷaṁ agādhanadīnada-
dustaram appa jaladurgada mahimeyumaṁ abhraṅkaṣaśikhariśikharadurllaṅghyamappa
giridurgada pempumaṁ udagratarugahanaduṣpravēśam appa vanadurgadunnatiyumaṁ
oḷakoṇḍu, nirantarāṭṭāḷakapratōḷīndrakauśaḷadēvapathasanāthaṅgaḷuṁ gaṇḍa-
śaiḷābhīḷaśiḷāyantrabhayaṅkaraṅgaḷuṁ praḷayakāḷānaḷavarṣaśaṅkākārihutava-
havarṣāgniyantrabhayānakaṅgaḷuṁ kaṇṭakagulmaviṣavallīsaṅghātabhīṣaṇaṅgaḷuṁ
jānubhañjaniśūlaprakaraparivr̥taṅgaḷuṁ kūpakūṭāvapātalōhakaṇṭakasaṅkaṭaṅgaḷuṁ
[p. 288]
tāḷapatraśr̥ṅgāṭakanicitaṅgaḷuṁ śvadaṁṣṭrārgaḷōparimasañchannaṅgaḷuṁ yantrāyudhā-
varaṇōpakaraṇapariṇataṅgaḷāgirda durgaṅgaḷoḷ,

ghanadōrdaṇḍaprabhāvārjitadharaṇiguhāsiṁharir nīmumīgaḷ

antītana kaṭakakke nityakṣayavyayapratyavāyaṅgaḷaṁ māḍi bēsaṟisi neladiṁ
teraḷcuvamalladoḍaṁ namma kuladēvategaḷ appa mēghamukhar emba nāgarājaremba
nāgarājarindamītanaḷurkeyumanurkumaṁ kiḍisi gelvam endu nuḍida mantrigaḷa-

mēkappud’ endu,

jaḷadākāradoḷeyde parbi sakaḷāśācakramuṁ vyōmamaṁ
ḍaḷamuṁ kargi kaṟaṅgi tōṟe siḍiliṁ miñciṁ ghanadhvānadiṁ
diḷe kampaṅgoḷe sōneyiṁ sarigaḷiṁ tandalgaḷindandu bhū

antu viḷayakāḷajaḷadōdīrṇajaḷamumaniḷisi jaḷadharajaḷadhiya naḍuve,

aḍiyoḷ pāsida car‍maratnapaṭamaṁ tacchatraratnaṁ beḍaṁ
giḍidōrantire muṭṭi polda teṟadindimbāge tanmadhyadoḷ
soḍarirpantire cakraratnamadaṟoḷ nirbādhamirdattu pe
rvaḍe vārāśiyoḷirda baitradoḷagandettaṁ teraḷdirdavol // Ādi.13.60 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

antu kr̥takacaturdvāradantarbhāgadoḷ sēnādhinātharakṣitam appa kaṭakakke

sthapatiratnaviracitāmbaragōcararathanikaraṅgaḷuṁ vajrada giḍigegaḷuṁ berasu mēgha-

tamadoḍḍirpavolirpa kārmugila taḷtoḍḍellamaṁ munnama

[p. 289]
siḍiliṁ miñciṁ moḻagiṁ
paḍeguḷkaṁ paḍevahīndrarerdegiḍuvinegaṁ

kaḍukeydānire cakravartivaregaṁ mēghāmarar barpareṁ

āgaḷā negaḻda samarakaḷakaḷamaṁ kēḷdidēnendu bharatēśvaracakravarti khaḍgaratnakke

gaṇabaddhāmarahūṅkr̥taṁ jayakumārōnmucyamānōgramā
rgaṇamā vīraninādasiṁhaninadaṁ tammaṁ paḷañcalke ta
tphaṇivr̥ndaṁ maṇidōḍe māṇade ciḷātāvartaraḷkutte kī
ḻmaṇidinnendudanembevendeṟagidar cakrēśapādābjadoḷ // Ādi.13.67 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

āgaḷ jayana bhujavijayasūcakam āgi mēghanādasamānam āda
siṁhanādakke cakravarti mecci mēghasvaranāmamaṁ vīrāgragaṇyapadaviyaṁ dayeg’ eydu
[p. 290]
ciḷātāvartara kuladhanamumaṁ yaśōdhanamumaṁ kaikoṇḍu avaraṁ vaśavidhē-
yar‍māḍi sindhunadītīrambiḍidu pōgi himavatparvatada sindhuprapātaman eydi
tanna baravanaṟididirvanda sindhudēviyindaṁ sindhujaḷaṅgaḷoḷabhiṣiktan āgi
bhadrāsanamaṁ paḍedu sindhudēviyanirisi katipayaprayāṇaṅgaḷiṁ himavanmadhyakūṭābhi-
mukhapradēśadoḷ bīḍaṁ biṭṭu niyamasthan āgi himavatkumāranumaṁ vijayārdha-
kumāranandadoḷe sādhisuvudumātanandōlagisida gōśīrṣacandanadivyauṣadhi-
māḷādi tadgirisamudbhūtasāravastugaḷaṁ kaikoṇḍu ājñāvidhēyar‍māḍi sindhunadī-
tīrambiḍidu pōgi himavatparvatamaṁ nōḍi,

idu haimādrīndramāṟuṁ kulagirige modal mēruśailēndramaṁ me

doreyalladaṅge nuḍivudu

eralege pāḍuva gōriya
naraṇyadoḷ mr̥gavirōdhigaṁ pāḍuvudē // Ādi.14.80 [kandaṁ]

bharatanum ene doregevandoḍāraḷavumanī

ad’ alladeyum udāravīracaritaniratakadanakarkaśakṣatriyaṅge vipakṣakṣatriya-

dhananāgal ninna tammaṁ ninageṟaganidaṁ nambu rājādhirājā // Ādi.14.84 [mahāsragdhare]

[p. 311]

rōdōntaṁ kūḍe ratnōjjvaḷagirikuḷadiṁ tūntaniṭṭante nīlāṁ

paribhavamaṁ cakravartigittattāgaḷ // Ādi.14.108 [kandaṁ]

antu ṣaṭkhaṇḍabharatamaṇḍaḷamanuṇḍigesādhyaṁ māḍi padineṇṭu kōṭi-
jātyaśvaṅgaḷumembattanālkulakke gandhasindhuraṅgaḷ appa bhadrahastigaḷumembattanālkulakke

mūvattirchāsirbar pratyantarājatanūjeyaruṁ mūvattirchāsirbaravarōdha-

doḍananēkadhānyasadanaṅgaḷuṁ kṣaumadukūlādi divyavasana vividhaprāvaraṇa-
viśēṣaṅgaḷuṁ nītiśāstraṅgaḷoḍananēkaśāstraṅgaḷuṁ strīpuruṣayōgyamaṇi-
muktābharaṇaṅgaḷuṁ cakravartiyājñeyindaṁ nelanellaṁ bandu koḷvoḍaṁ tavada
kanakarāśiyuṁ marakatapadmarāgavajravaiḍūryamuktāphaḷādinavaratnaṅgaḷumanukrama-
dindaṁ śrīgr̥hadoḷ puṭṭida kāḷamahākāḷanaisarpapāṇḍukapadmapiṅgaḷa-
māṇavakaśaṅkhasarvaratnaṅgaḷ emba navanidhigaḷuṁ āyudhāgāradoḷ puṭṭida
cakrāsidaṇḍacchatraratnaṅgaḷuṁ śrīgr̥hadoḷ puṭṭida nidhimaṇicarmakākiṇī ratnaṅgaḷuṁ,
vijayārdhaparvatadoḷ puṭṭida gajāśvastrīratnaṅgaḷuṁ sākētanagaradoḷ puṭṭida
sēnānāyakapurōhitagr̥hapatitakṣakaratnaṅgaḷuṁ antu padinālkuṁ teṟada jīvājīva-
ratnaṅgaḷuṁ kṣitisāram emba prākāradoḷaṁ sarvatōbhadram emba gōpuradoḷaṁ
kūḍida vaijayantiy emba divyaprāsādamuṁ diksvastikam emba sabhābhūmiyuṁ
nandyāvartam emba śibiranivēśamuṁ girikūṭam emba digavalōkanagr̥hamuṁ
vardhamānamembīkṣaṇapriyaprēkṣāgr̥hamuṁ mahāgharmāntam emba dhārāgr̥hamuṁ
gr̥hakūṭam emba varṣāvāsamuṁ puṣkaḷāvatiy emba śayanasadanamuṁ

jīmūtam emba majjanagr̥hamuṁ avataṁsikey emba ratnamāleyuṁ dēvaramyamemba
paṭakuṭiyuṁ siṁhavidhr̥tam appa siṁhavāhiniy emba mr̥duśayyeyuṁ mēru
kaṇṭhōpamam emba siṁhāsanamuṁ, yakṣakaravidhūyamānamappanupamamaṅgaḷamemba

[p. 327]
ratnamuṁ subhadrey emba strīratnamuṁ dvādaśayōjanasaṁsarpanninādaṅgaḷappānandi-
gaḷ emba panneraḍuṁ mahābhērigaḷuṁ vijayaghōṣaṅgaḷ emba panneraḍuṁ paṭahaṅgaḷuṁ
puṇyābdhisambhavaṅgaḷ āgi gambhīrāvartaṅgaḷembirpattanālkuṁ śaṅkhaṅgaḷuṁ nālvatteṇṭu
kōṭi patākegaḷuṁ taṭidvaḷayaviḷasitaṅgaḷ āgi nijaprakōṣṭhaniṣṭhitaṅgaḷ appa vīrāṅgadaṁ
gaḷ emba kaṭakaṅgaḷuṁ mahākalyāṇakārakam emba divyāhāramuṁ amr̥tagarbhaṅgaḷemba
sadyōghr̥tamuṁ amr̥taparimaḷāmōdam emba dadhiyuṁ amr̥tarasāyanamemba
pānamuṁ mattaṁ mūvattirchāsiraviṣayaṅgaḷuṁ eḻpattirchāsirapoḻalgaḷuṁ
tombattāṟu kōṭigrāmaṅgaḷuṁ padināṟusāsira khēḍaṅgaḷuṁ padināṟusāsira-
saṁvāhanaṅgaḷuṁ aivattāṟantaradvīpaṅgaḷuṁ ēkakōṭipramāṇasthāligaḷuṁ
śatasahasrakōṭihalaṅgaḷuṁ mūṟukōṭigōmaṇḍaḷamuṁ pratyantavāsigaḷappē-
ḻnūṟukukṣinivāsigaḷuṁ eḻpattirchāsiradurgāṭavigaḷuṁ padineṇchāsira mlēccharājaruṁ
ātmīyasāmrājyaparicchēdamāge vajravr̥ṣabhanārācaśarīrasaṁhananasaumyanuṁ
samacaturasrasaṁsthānanuṁ niṣṭaptakanakavarṇanuṁ svastika nandyāvartādi catuṣṣaṣṭilakṣaṇa-
dharanuṁ tiḷamasūrikādyanēkavyañjananidhiyuṁ apāravīr‍yanuṁ pañcaśatacāpōtsē-
dhanuṁ caturaśītilakṣaṇapūrvānapavartyāyuṣyanuṁ apratihataśāsananumāgi,

himadindaṁ lavaṇāmburāśivaregaṁ ṣaṭkhaṇḍabhūmaṇḍaḷaṁ
nimirdājñāprasarakkagurvugoḷeyuṁ vidyādharar māgadhā
dyamarar tannane niccamōlagiseyuṁ cakrēśvaraṁ kīrtivi
bhramadiṁ pajjaḷipannamujjaḷisidaṁ vyōmāvanībhāgamaṁ // Ādi.15.4 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

antu bharataṁ bharatamaṇḍaḷamanēkacchatracchāyeyindaṁ pratipālisuttu-
mireyire,

puranidhiśayyāsanarā
jyaratnavāhanavarūthinīnāṭyasabhā
parikarasahitaṁ bharatē
śvaraṅge samasandudī daśāṅgaṁ bhōgaṁ // Ādi.15.5 [kandaṁ]

int’ ayōdhyāsiṁhāsanāsīnanumuditōditasāmrājyasukhānubhavanuṁ
kr̥takr̥tyanum appa sakalacakravarti,

jinapūjōtsavamaṁ mahāmahamumaṁ tāṁ māḍi salvannegaṁ
dhanamaṁ takkavargīyavēḻpudadanantēgeydumollar tapō

[p. 328]
dhanarārādhyagr̥hastharādaroḷaminnār takkarāraiveno
yyanupāyāntaradindamendosageyaṁ tadvyājadiṁ māḍidaṁ // Ādi.15.6 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

antu māḍi,

haritāṅkuraphaḷapuṣpō
tkaraṅgaḷaṁ posate moḷeta dhānyaṅgaḷanā
dharaṇīśaṁ kedaṟisidaṁ
nirantaraṁ rājagēhadoḷagaṁ poṟagaṁ // Ādi.15.7 [kandaṁ]

kedaṟisi baḻiyaṁ baravē
ḻvudumalli kelar vivēkarahitar bandar
modaloḷe pokkar bratami
lladavar taḻiyuttumaṅkuraṅgaḷanāgaḷ // Ādi.15.8 [kandaṁ]

sāvadyabhīrugaḷ kela
rā vividhaphalaprasūnapallavatatiyiṁ
tīvida rājāṅgaṇamani
ḷāvandyar meṭṭalolladalliye nindar // Ādi.15.9 [kandaṁ]

nilaloḍamanibarumaṁ bhū
talapati baḻiyaṭṭi barise peṟat’ ond’ eḍeyoḷ
malarahitar bandu dharā
lalanādhīśaṅge vinatamastakarādar // Ādi.15.10 [kandaṁ]

āgaḷ bharatēśvaracakravarti nīminibarumivar banda mārgadoḷ
bārade peṟatondu mārgadoḷēke bandirendu besagoḷe,

phaḷakusumapravāḷaharitāṅkurarājiyoḷalli jīvasaṁ
kuḷamaḷavalladuṇṭadaṟināgadu parvadinaṅgaḷoḷ brataṁ
gaḷanoḍagūḍi nindemage meṭṭaliḷēśvara kēḷdevāvidaṁ
tiḷiye gaṇādhipar besase rundrajinēndrasabhāntarāḷadoḷ // Ādi.15.11 [campakamāle]

adaṟiṁ pravāḷapatrapuṣpāṅkuraṅgaḷindaṁ saṅkīrṇam appa rājāṅgaṇamaṁ
meṭṭade peṟatonde baṭṭeyoḷ bandevembuduṁ nābhinandananandananavara dr̥ḍhavratakke
mecci dānasanmānayōgyarappar endu padmanidhiy emba nidhiyaṁ tarisi tapanīya
[p. 329]
sūtradoḷēkādyēkōttaradaśāntambaramavaravara nelegaḷoḷ brahmasūtrābhidhāna-
yajñōpavītadiṁ pavitragātrar‍ māḍi,

ēnabhimatamavargavargada
nēnuṁ todaḷilladittu mannisidaṁ sa
nmānapurassaramantuṭe
nānāvratayutaranārumēṁ mannisarē // Ādi.15.12 [kandaṁ]

bratahīnarananibarumaṁ
kṣitipati bēṟirisi mānyaraṁ mannise ta
dvratahīnarumandakhiḷa
bratamaṁ kaikoḷva bagege bageyaṁ tandar // Ādi.15.13 [kandaṁ]

bharatēśvaraṁ tānuṁ munne bhaṭṭārakara samakṣadoḷ samākarṇi-
tōpāsakādhyayananappudaṟindamārēnaṁ bēḻparavargadane koṭṭu cakravartigaḷ
māḻpa kalpavr̥kṣamuṁ mahāmaṇḍaḷikapramukhamakuṭabaddhar māḻpa caturmukhamuṁ
ardhamaṇḍaḷikar māḻpa sarvatōbhadram emba pesaranoḍeya mahāmahamuṁ
indrar māḻpa indradhvajamuṁ samastabhavyajananirvartyamānāṣṭāhnikamuṁ
caityālayanir‍māṇanirmāpaṇaśāsanārōpitagrāmakṣētravitaraṇamuṁ munijana-
pūjānnadānādikaraṇajinagr̥hajanasatatōpanīyamāna pādyagandhākṣatakusumacaru-
dhūpadīpaphalādyarcanātmakam appa nityamahamuṁ śāntikapauṣṭikādigaḷumaṁ bagedu
māḻpa baliyuṁ ghr̥takṣīradadhināḷikēratōyāmrarasēkṣurasagandhōdakādigaḷiṁ
māḍuva savanamuṁ mūṟuṁ pottumarcanāpurassaraṁ dhūpōddhāraṅgeyva nirantara-
trisandhyāsēveyumendeṇṭu teṟada pūjeyumanarkapūjeyumaṁ mannisi asimaṣi-
kr̥ṣivaṇigvidyāśilpakar‍maṅgaḷiṁ śuddhavr̥ttiyindarthōpārjanaṅgeyva vārteyuṁ
triśuddhiyinanukampeverasu samastaprāṇigaḷgabhayaṅguḍuva dayādattiyuṁ kriyāmantraṁ
gaḷindamātmasamānaśrāvakāgraṇigaḷge kanyābhūmisuvarṇahastyaśvaratharatnādigaḷaṁ kuḍuva
samadattiyuṁ paramatapaścaraṇaniratayatisamitigellaṁ pratigrahādi purassaraṁ niravadyā-
hārādivitaraṇarūpa pātradattiyuṁ nijānvayōddharaṇasamarthanappagratanūbha-
vaṅgātmīyadhar‍madhanabandhugaḷaṁ samarpipa sakaḷadattiyuṁ berasu caturvidhamappa
dattiyuṁ upāsakādhyayanādhyāpanānantaraṁ sakaḷaśāstraṅgaḷanōduvōdisuva neneva
bareva paramasvādhyāyamuṁ pañcāṇuvratādipravartanasvabhāvasaṁyamamuṁ anaśana-
vr̥ttyādi tapōnuṣṭhānumuṁ berasāryaṣaṭkarmaṅgaḷaṁ nimagivu kulācāraṁ
gaḷendaṟiye pēḻdu kaikoḷisi,


[p. 330]
āṟuṁ vr̥ttigaḷanivaṁ
mīṟidarallar dvijanmarī vr̥ttigaḷiṁ
bēṟādar dvijaruntēṁ
bēṟuṇṭe manuṣyajāti tānonde valaṁ // Ādi.15.14 [kandaṁ]

vratasaṁskāradinādar
vitataguṇar brāhmaṇar kriyāsantatisaṁ
yutarucitasatkriyāvira
hitanātaṁ nāmadhārakaṁ dvijanallaṁ // Ādi.15.15 [kandaṁ]

end’ avaranātmīyānvayōcitavrataṅgaḷoḷ dr̥ḍhavrataraṁ māḍi mattaṁ
dvādaśāṅgaṅgaḷoḷ pēḻdādhānaprītisuprītidhr̥timōdapriyōdbhavanāmakar‍ma-
bahiryānaniṣadyānnaprāśanavyuṣṭikēśāvāpa lipisaṅkhyāna saṅgrahōpanayanabrata-
car‍yāvratāvataraṇa vivāhavarṇalābhakulacaryā gr̥hīśitvapraśāntigr̥hatyāga dīkṣā-
dyajinarūpatāmaunādhyayanavr̥ttatva tīrthakr̥dbhāvanāgurusthānābhyupagama-
gaṇōpagrahaṇasvagurusthānasaṅkrāntinissaṅgatvātmabhāvanāyōganirvāṇasamprāpti-
yōganir‍vāṇasādhanēndrōpapādābhiṣēkavidhidānasukhōdayēndratyā-
gāvatārahiraṇyagarbhōtkr̥ṣṭajanmatāmandarādrīndrābhiṣēkagurupūjōpa-
lambhanayauvarājya svarājyacakralābhadigvijayacakrābhiṣēkasāmrājya pariniṣkramaṇa-
yōgasammahārhantyavihārayōgatyāgāgranirvr̥tiyembayvattumūṟu
garbhādinirvāṇapar‍yantaṅgaḷ appa garbhānvayakriyegaḷaṁ

modaliṁ taguḷdu tudivara
midarkidācāraṇamidaṟa vidhiyintuṭu ta
ppade mantrapūrvakaṁ nega
ḻvudendu cakrādhipaṁ manaṅgoḷe pēḻdaṁ // Ādi.15.16 [kandaṁ]

mattam avatāravr̥tti lōbhasthānalābhagaṇagrahaṇapūjārādhyapuṇyayajña-
car‍yōpayōgatvamembeṇṭu berasuṁ pūrvōktōpanayanādicatvāriṁśatkriye-
gaḷoḍane nālvatteṇṭudīkṣānvayakriyegaḷumaṁ sajjātisadgr̥hatvapārivrājyapada surēndratva-
sāmrājyaparamārhantyaparinir‍vāṇamembēḻuṁ paramasthānanāmakartranvaya-
kriyegaḷanatibālavidyākulāvadhivarṇōttamatvapātratvasr̥ṣṭyadhikāra vyavahārēśitvā-
vadhyatvādaṇḍyatvamānārhatvaprajāsambandhāntaram emba pattumadhikāraṅgaḷumanaṟipi,
mattaṁ garbhānvayādikriyegaḷananuṣṭhisuvāgaḷ vinēyajanatāsatatārjita jinabhavana
[p. 331]
doḷamātmīyagr̥hābhyantarapraśastapradēśagaḷoḷaṁ praśastamr̥ttikāviracitōnnata-
vēdītaḷāṣṭamahāpratihār‍yasamanvitajagatpūjyapūjitārhatpratimegaḷaṁ niṟisi
yathāśaktisnapanapūjāpurassaraṁ bahuvidhārcanegaḷindarcisi dharmacakracchatratritayaṅgaḷaṁ
baḷasiyumupāśrayambaḍeye niṟisi tīr‍thakaragaṇadharānagārakēvaḷigaḷa parinirvāṇa-
kṣētradoḷ śarīrasaṁskārādigārhapatyadakṣiṇāgnyāhavanīyam emba pesaraṁ paḍedagni-
trayaṅgaḷoḷagarhadarcanāśēṣaghr̥tatiḷājyāhutigaḷinupāsakādhyayanagadita samasta-
prakāra pipīlikājātyādimantraṅgaḷiṁ kriyānuyuktamāge pēḻdu pūr‍vāpara-
vidēhaṅgaḷoḷ avyavacchinnarūpadiṁ bharatairāvataṅgaḷoḷ nijōcitakāla-
kālārambhāvasānarūpadiṁ negaḻdī kriyāviśēṣaṅgaḷanillinditteḍeyuḍugade
naḍeyisuvudu; ī kriyegaḷanuṣṭhānamantraśūnyaṅgaḷāgadandu,

dorekoḷipuvu tatkriyeyoḷ
pariṇamisuva phalamanastraśastratanutrō
tkararahitaṅgasahāyaṁ
garātibaḷajayamanaḷavu dorekoḷisuvavōl // Ādi.15.17 [kandaṁ]

adaṟindaṁ sakaḷāgama
vidaridaniṁ tappadantu negaḻiṁ negaḻdaṁ
duditōditaparamasukhā
spadakke bagedante nīve modaligarappir // Ādi.15.18 [kandaṁ]

idanādiprabhavaṁ bhavabhramaṇaduḥkhōgrāgniyoḷ maḻgida
ppudu jīvaṅgaḷanembinaṁ baḷasadī mithyātvabandhaṁ kaḻa
ldudiruttirpinegaṁ caturdaśaguṇasthānaṅgaḷaṁ nambi po
rdidavar pordidaralte muktivanitākāñcīguṇasthānamaṁ // Ādi.15.19 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

paramabrahmatanūbhavar dvijavarar varṇōttamar lōkapū
jyariḷāvallabhamānyarunnataguṇar cāritraśuddhar dharā
mararī brāhmaṇarendu koṇḍukonedā ṣaṭkhaṇḍabhūmaṇḍalē
śvaranōrante negaḻce kūḍe negaḻdattettaṁ dvijanmānvayaṁ // Ādi.15.20 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

end’ intu nābhinandana
nandananānandadindamandavaraṁ ta
nnendandadinde naḍeyisi
daṁ dānaṅguḍuvadondalampina pempiṁ // Ādi.15.21 [kandaṁ]


[p. 332]
antu bharatēśvaraṁ bharatakṣētradoḷ tāne māḍida tanna koṇḍāṭa-
dinatiprasiddhamāda viprasantati kelavukālaṁ naḍevannegamondudivasaṁ triyāmā-
virāmadoḷ āścar‍yabhūtaṅgaḷuṁ dūrāriṣṭaphalasūcakaṅgaḷum appa svapnaṅgaḷaṁ kaṇḍu
bercidanterdumīgaḷenna kaṇḍa kanasugaḷī yugada kaḍeyoḷ prajegaḷge vividhōpadrava-
sūcakaṅgaḷ āgi tōrkumendanumānadinaspaṣṭarūpadinaṟidu bhagavadarhatsamīpakke
pōgi yugapatsakaḷapadārthayathārthāvabhāsiy appa kēvalajñānadiṁ viśēṣaniścayamaṁ
māḍuvanendu sakaḷa prābhātikakriyeyaṁ nirvartisi makuṭabaddhaparivr̥tan āgi bandu
kaiḷāsagirīndrasthitasamavasr̥tiyaṁ saṁsr̥tilatāvicchēdiyaṁ pokku gandhakuṭiyaṁ
mūṟusūḻbalavandu dēvadānavagandharvavidyādharārādhyanaṁ vr̥ṣabhanāthananarthānu-
gatāṣṭōttarasahasranāmāṅkitastutigaḷiṁ stutiyisi divyārcanegaḷindarcisi gaṇadharādi-
yatisamitigeṟagi nijōcitasthānadoḷ kuḷḷirdāgaḷ,

pariṇāmaśuddhi dorekoḷe
puruparamēśvarapadābjabhaktiya bharadiṁ
bharataṅge śāstralakṣaṇa
parikaradiṁ toṭṭanavadhi puṭṭittāgaḷ // Ādi.15.22 [kandaṁ]

ant’ utpannāvadhibōdhaṁ dhar‍māmr̥tāsvādanaparan āgi kiṟidu pottan irdu
nijamanōgatakār‍yavijñāpanamukharamukhan āgi,

ādibrahmanenal moda
lādudaṟiṁ dēva māḻpa nīnirdantā
nāda maruḷtanadindu
tpādisideṁ bratasamētaviprānvayamaṁ // Ādi.15.23 [kandaṁ]

guṇabhūmivibhāgadoḷā
deṇikeyoḷondādiyāge pannonduvaraṁ
guṇavadbratacihnaṁ guṇa
maṇibhūṣaṇasūtramamarduvavargennindaṁ // Ādi.15.24 [kandaṁ]

idaṟoḷ guṇamō dōṣamo
podaḷdu nindapudayuktamō yuktamo pē
ḻidu hāniyo vr̥ddhiyo tā
nadāvudaṁ pordi nilkumaghavighaṭapaṭū // Ādi.15.25 [kandaṁ]


[p. 333]
ad’ alladeyum indina dinaṁ beḷag appa jāvadoḷ padināṟu kanasugaḷaṁ
kaṇḍenā kanasugaḷaniṣṭaphalasūcakaṅgaḷembudaṁ sāmānyadinupalakṣisidenavaṟa
phalamumanenagaṟiye besasimendavadhijñānadiṁ tānā kanasugaḷanaṟivanāgiyuṁ
sabhājanakkamaṟipalendu besagoḷvuduṁ praśnānukramadiṁ trilōkaguruvintendu
besasidaṁ nīnā dvijanmajātiyaṁ oḷḷitaṁ māḍideyādoḍaṁ,

dhareyoḷ dhar‍mārthadiṁ nīṁ sr̥jiyisi negaḻdī viprasantānadondā
caraṇaṁ nīnenda pāṅgiṁ kr̥tayugadoḷe dalsalguminnatta naṣṭā
caraṇaṁ sanmārgadoḷ maccarisi kaliyugābhyarṇadoḷ dravyalōbhā
turarunmārgōpadēśōdyatamatigaḷatikrūrarappar dvijanmar // Ādi.15.26 [mahāsragdhare]

madhumadyamāṁsalōlupa
radhār‍mikar paravadhūratipriyaradhamar
vadhaniratar pāpigaḷanr̥
tadhanar dvijarinnarapparā kaliyugadoḷ // Ādi.15.27 [kandaṁ]

ādoḍam īgaḷavar sadācārarappudaṟiṁ avaranā māḻkeyoḷe
naḍeyalīyade māḍi kiḍisidoḍe ninage piriduṁ dūṟakkum endu pēḻdu mattamātana
kaṇḍa ṣōḍaśasvapnasūcitaphalaṅgaḷanint’ endu besasidar -

bharatamahītaḷamanaḷaṁ
karisirdirpattanālku kēsarigaḷanā
daradiṁ kaṇḍudaṟindani
bare tīrthakararkaḷapparavara vihāraṁ // Ādi.15.28 [kandaṁ]

dhareyoḷ sale pāṣaṇḍiga
ḷarebar puṭṭiyumaḍaṅguvar mattaṁ kē
sarigaḷa baḷasiyumanukū
larūpadāḍuva mr̥gaṅgaḷaṁ kaṇḍudaṟiṁ // Ādi.15.29 [kandaṁ]

paramajinatīrtharoḷ pala
barumāgiyumēṁ kuliṅgigaḷ vikr̥tigaḷiṁ
virahitarappar madasiṁ
dhurabhāramanānalāṟadaḷpiṁ bennaṁ // Ādi.15.30 [kandaṁ]


[p. 334]
naḷinaḷidu naḍeva hayadaḻi
yaḷavaṁ kaṇḍudaṟinadhikabalamunipadhr̥tā
tuḷaguṇabhāramanāmpani
taḷavillade kiḍuvaralte duṣṣamayatigaḷ // Ādi.15.31 [kandaṁ]

neredondi ninda śākvara
varayūthamanavaninātha kaṇḍudaṟindo
rvare viharipudaṁ bisuṭaṁ
barāmbarar tamma samudayamberasirpar // Ādi.15.32 [kandaṁ]

musuṟida mugilgaḷindaṇa
meseyade nindarkabimbamaṁ kaṇḍudaṟiṁ
deseyadu duṣṣamakālado
ḷasadr̥śakaivalyabōdhadinakarabimbaṁ // Ādi.15.33 [kandaṁ]

kaḷikāṅkurakusumōtkara
phaḷapallavarahitamahijamaṁ kaṇḍudaṟiṁ
daḷavillada naranārī
kuḷamanupamasatyaśaucavirahitamakkuṁ // Ādi.15.34 [kandaṁ]

haritāṅkurapallavapa
trarājiyaṁ bisuṭu śuṣkapatraṅgaḷanā
daradiṁ mēvajakuḷamaṁ
dorekoḷe nīṁ svapnakāladoḷ kaṇḍudaṟiṁ // Ādi.15.35 [kandaṁ]

samayigaḷuṁ cāturva
rṇamumucitacaritramaṁ bisuṭṭādaṁ po
llameyoḷ sale naḍevar du
ṣṣamamembaydaneya kāladoḷ bharatanr̥pā // Ādi.15.36 [kandaṁ]

karipatiyanēṟi kōḍaga
mire kaṇḍudaṟindamādibhūpar kiḍe bē
ḍarumakulīnarumatidu
ścaritraruṁ bhūparapparanyāyaparar // Ādi.15.37 [kandaṁ]

gūgegaḷaṁ kaṇḍey appa kāraṇadiṁ jai
nāgamavidaraṁ sārade
pōgi kuliṅgigaḷanī janaṁ sēvisuguṁ // Ādi.15.38 [kandaṁ]

āḍuva maruḷgaḷaṁ naḍe
nōḍidudaṟinintu kanasinoḷ makkaḷgaṁ
kūḍe pesariṭṭu sale koṁ
ḍāḍidapar vyantararkaḷaṁ jaḍamatigaḷ // Ādi.15.39 [kandaṁ]

kaḍeviḍidu baḷasi nīrire
naḍubattida keṟeyanintu kaṇḍudaṟindaṁ
naḍunāḍoḷaṟaṁ nelasade
kaḍeyoḷ nelegoḷgumilli sandeyamuṇṭē // Ādi.15.40 [kandaṁ]

dhūḷīdhūsaravarara
tnāḷigaḷaṁ kaṇḍa dūsaṟindaṁ dharaṇī
pāḷakamunipar pañcama
kāḷadoḷaṇamāgaralte r̥ddhiprāptar // Ādi.15.41 [kandaṁ]

koraloḷ kaṭṭida māleya
sirikhaṇḍada taḷkuverasu biḍunāybesedā
daradindanarghyamaṇivi
ṣṭaradoḷ kuḷḷirdu saruganuṇe kaṇḍudaṟiṁ // Ādi.15.42 [kandaṁ]

vratahīnar sanmārga
pratikūlar vyasanavaśagatar pāpigaḷiṁ
tatikaṣṭarapparavaniyo
ḷatithi[ga]ḷinnannadānamaṁ kuḍuveḍeyoḷ // Ādi.15.43 [kandaṁ]

taruṇavr̥ṣaṁ keledu toḻa
ltare kaṇḍudaṟinde jainadīkṣege meyyaṁ
taruṇajanaṅgaḷe tarpar
pariṇatavayasarkaḷappavar meydārar // Ādi.15.44 [kandaṁ]


[p. 336]
parivēṣaṅgoṇḍa niśā
karanaṁ kaṇḍudaṟinandu muninikarakkā
daradavadhimanaḥpar‍yaya
meraḍumaṇaṁ puṭṭavendu nambu narēndrā // Ādi.15.45 [kandaṁ]

pudida taṟagelegaḷaṁ kaṁ
ḍudaṟindaṁ dhānyasamiti nīrasamakkuṁ
tudiyoḷ manujapratatiga
made dal bhōgōpabhōgakāraṇamakkuṁ // Ādi.15.46 [kandaṁ]

ivu dūraphalaṅgaḷ sva
pnaviśēṣaṅgaḷ tanūja kokkarisadiri
nnivaṟeḍege ninage sale mā
ḻke viśvavighnōpaśāntiyaṁ jinadhar‍maṁ // Ādi.15.47 [kandaṁ]

embuduṁ bharatēśvaraṁ prasannamanan āgi vr̥ṣabhasēnādyanupama paryanta-
gaṇadharadēvacaritākarṇanamane tanage karṇapūrammāḍi bhagavatsiṁhāsanaratna-
raśmicchaṭātipūtabhūtaḷakke,

kusumōpahāramesevaṁ
tesevinamā namramauḷiśēkharavigaḷa
tkusumōtkaranarghyayaśaḥ
kusumitadiglatikaneṟagidaṁ bharatēśaṁ // Ādi.15.48 [kandaṁ]

antu puruparamēśvaraṅgeṟagi bandayōdhyāpuramaṁ pokku dussvapna-
darśanakarṣaṇārtham āgi kalpavr̥kṣamahāmahimāpurassaraṁ bhagavadarhadabhiṣēka-
munipūjanasatpātradānapraṇayaprīṇanamāhāravitaraṇagōdōhaplavāvanītaḷa-
santarpaṇādi śāntikakriyegaḷaṁ negaḻdu,

vividhadvīpaṅgaḷoḷ mandaragiritaṭadoḷ jyōtirāvāsadoḷ dē
vavimānānīkadoḷ śōbhisuva jinagr̥havrātamaṁ geldu ratna
cchaviyiṁ digbhittiyaṁ citrisuva jinanikētaṅgaḷaṁ māḍisuttuṁ
divijēndrastutyanādaṁ sukavijanamanōmānasōttaṁsahaṁsaṁ // Ādi.15.49 [mahāsragdhare]

ant’ ayōdhyāpurōpāntakāntapradēśaṅgaḷoḷaṁ kaiḷāsōdagra-
kūṭaṅgaḷoḷaṁ ṣaṭkhaṇḍamaṇḍaḷaprasiddharājadhānigaḷoḷaṁ,


[p. 337]
desegaḷ percade moṭṭanāduvagalakkembannegaṁ nīḷamā
gasadoḷ kāḷasegoṇḍudembinegamadrīndraṅgaḷaṁ tandu kī
lisidaṁ niścaḷamappinaṁ vasudhegākalpāntamembantu mā
ḍisidaṁ jainagr̥haṅgaḷaṁ palavumaṁ saṁsārasārōdayaṁ // Ādi.15.50 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]


idu dēvēndramunīndravandyaparamajinēndramukhacandra
vākcandrikāprasaraprasādōdīrṇasūktikallōlamālākīrṇa

pañcadaśāśvāsaṁ

[p. 338]
[ṣōḍaśāśvāsaṁ]

śrīramaṇīniḷayajinā
gāraṅgaḷ tanna jasadavol vasudhegaḷaṁ
kāraṅgaḷāge pūrṇama
nōrathanādaṁ sarasvatīmaṇihāraṁ // Ādi.16.1 [kandaṁ]

antu tanna māḍisida caityālayaṅgaḷoḷ ādibhaṭṭārakādiyāge
bhaviṣyattīrthakarapratikr̥tigaḷaṁ pañcaratnamayaṅgaḷaṁ māḍisi māṇikyadēvarendu
koṇḍāḍi tatpūjākaraṇapuṇyavāsaraṅgaḷoḷ upavāsaniratanaparimitājya-
kṣīradadhināḷikērasahakārapūgīphalapuṇḍrēkṣurasaṅgaḷindaṁ gōśīrṣacandanakarpūra-
parimaḷasurabhigandhōdakaṅgaḷindamabhiṣēkaṅgeydu,

phaḷadoḷ dēvēndranudyānada vividhaphalaṁ pūgaḷoḷ kalpavr̥kṣaṁ
gaḷa pūgaḷ dīpadoḷ pannagapatiya phaṇāratnadīpaṁ vitānā
vaḷiyoḷ divyaṁ vitānaṁ tuṟugidavamarēndrārcanakkintidāyta
ggaḷamembantāge divyārcaneyoḷe meṟedaṁ bhaktiyaṁ cakranāthaṁ // Ādi.16.2 [mahāsragdhare]

ant’ arcisi nirbharapraṇāmāñjalipraṇayakr̥tōttamāṅganāgi,

kamaḷāḷaṅkr̥tam appa hēmakamaḷaṁ māṇikyabhaṭṭāraka
dyumaṇijyōtiyinoyyanuḷḷalardavol celvembinaṁ bhavyahr̥
tkamaḷakkaṁ mudamaṁ japāprasavaraktāśōkabandhūkaśō
ṇamaṇijyōtigaḷekkeyiṁ kuḍe jayaṁ bhadraṁ śubhaṁ maṅgaḷaṁ // Ādi.16.3 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

kaṇi ratnatritayakkidēṁ piridenal ratnākaraṁ ratnatō
raṇaratnāsanaratnavibhramaṇaratnāśōkaratnaprabhā
maṇiratnātapavāraṇatritayadiṁ trailōkyasāmrājyabhū
ṣaṇamāṇikyajinēndrabimbame jayaṁ bhadraṁ śubhaṁ maṅgaḷaṁ // Ādi.16.4 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]


[p. 339]
paripūrṇōjjvalacandrabimbaruciyiṁ candraprabhaṁ puṣpadaṁ
tarenal gāruḍanīlaśōṇamaṇihēmacchāyeyindirpati

ttire māṇikyajinēndrabimbame jayaṁ bhadraṁ śubhaṁ maṅgaḷaṁ // Ādi.16.5 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

sphuritōdyatkanakaprabhāprasaradiṁ pītāmbaraṁ padmavi
ṣṭaradiṁ paṅkajaviṣṭaraṁ natavinēyavrātacētastamō
haranāgirdudaṟiṁ haraṁ bhavaharaṁ māṇikyadēvaṁ vasuṁ
dharegintorbane dēvanāgire jayaṁ bhadraṁ śubhaṁ maṅgaḷaṁ // Ādi.16.6 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

vipinōllaṅghanasindhuyānanagakūṭārōhaṇaklēśamaṁ
trapadadhyānabiḷapravēśarasavādāyāsadoḷ bārte tī
rdapudē pordaloḍaṁ vinēyajanasaṅghātakke māṇikyadē
vapadāmbhōjavaraprasādame jayaṁ bhadraṁ śubhaṁ maṅgaḷaṁ // Ādi.16.7 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

sakaḷakṣmācarakhēcarāñcitamahāmāṇikyagāṇikyahā
stikaratnōrjitacakravartivibhavaṁ munnaṁ baḻikkaindramai

tikamaṁ sāre vinēyarājige jayaṁ bhadraṁ śubhaṁ maṅgaḷaṁ // Ādi.16.8 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

kupitānēkapadandaśūkadavadaityārāticōrāndhakā
rapatadvajraviṣābhicārikajarātaṅkādibhēdaṅgaḷa
ppupasargaṅgaḷa nōvanāveḍeyoḷaṁ kaigāva māṇikyadē
vapadāmbhōjame bhavyakōṭige jayaṁ bhadraṁ śubhaṁ maṅgaḷaṁ // Ādi.16.9 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

sitadūrvāṅkuramātuluṅganaḷinībhr̥ṅgāragōrōcanā
kṣatadadhyādiviḍambamaṅgaḷadoḷēṁ saṁsāramaṁ dāṇṭuvū
rjitapuṇyaṅgapavargalakṣmivaregaṁ saṁsārasārōdayō
ditamāṇikyajinastavāvaḷi jayaṁ bhadraṁ śubhaṁ maṅgaḷaṁ // Ādi.16.10 [mattēbhavikrīḍitaṁ]

namō vr̥ṣabhanāthāya tasmai vismayakāriṇē
purāṇōऽpyadvitīyassan yugabhāraṁ babhāra yaḥ // Ādi.16.11 [anuṣṭubh]

namō ’punarbhavapluṣṭakandarpāya tapōऽgninā
bōdhadr̥ṣṭibhuvāऽścar‍yadhāmnā sambhavaśambhavē // Ādi.16.13 [anuṣṭubh]

namassamastajagatāmatyantasvāsthyahētavē
dhar‍macakrapavitrā[rci]rabhinandanaviṣṇavē // Ādi.16.14 [anuṣṭubh]

svātmōpalabdhamārgasya svayambōdhāt svayambhuvē // Ādi.16.15 [anuṣṭubh]

namaḥ padmaprabhēśāya tasmai padmaprabhāsinē
jagannamati kiṁ citraṁ janōdātta virajyatē // Ādi.16.16 [anuṣṭubh]

namaḥ supārśvanāthāya yaḥ pārśvadvayacāmaraiḥ
muktilakṣmīkaṭākṣairvā rējē dugdhacchaṭōjjvalaiḥ // Ādi.16.17 [anuṣṭubh]

namaḥ prakṣīṇarāgāya labdhātiśayaśuddhayē
satpathōddyōtinē nityaṁ candraprabhajinēndavē // Ādi.16.18 [anuṣṭubh]

namassuvidhayē yasya jagadgahanajr̥mbhitaḥ
syādvādasiṁhanādōbhūt saṅkucadvādikuñjaraḥ // Ādi.16.19 [anuṣṭubh]

namaśśītaḷanāthāya yatsūktāmr̥tapāyināṁ
prāṇināṁ vipralambhāya na bhōgamr̥gatr̥ṣṇikā // Ādi.16.20 [anuṣṭubh]

namaśśrēyō jinēndrāya yatpādāśrayavartināṁ
śrēyāṁsi bahuvighnānītyuktērarthō nirāśrayaḥ // Ādi.16.21 [anuṣṭubh]

namaḥ śrīvāsupūjyāya bhajatāṁ bhāvapūjayā
yō bhavēdvaradassatyaṁ bhaktyā tuṣyanti dēvatāḥ // Ādi.16.22 [anuṣṭubh]

namō vimalanāthāya yadbōdhasya samaṁ kr̥taṁ
sākṣādvibhāsi bhāvasya darpaṇapratimārpaṇaṁ // Ādi.16.23 [anuṣṭubh]

rajō yēna kṣaṇāddhautamadhyātmadhyānavāriṇā // Ādi.16.24 [anuṣṭubh]


[p. 341]

dharmō jayati nādharma ityamōghīkr̥taṁ vacaḥ // Ādi.16.25 [anuṣṭubh]

ṣaṭkhaṇḍarājyamatyākṣīdyōऽnanttaiśvar‍yakāṅkṣayā // Ādi.16.26 [anuṣṭubh]

rājāsannadbhutaṁ cakrē cakrāṅkakamalōtsavaṁ // Ādi.16.28 [anuṣṭubh]

bandhamōkṣavidhijñāya dadhatēऽnantavīr‍yatāṁ // Ādi.16.29 [anuṣṭubh]

uttaṁsitaṁ mahēndrēṇa mandāragalitādaraṁ // Ādi.16.31 [anuṣṭubh]

namaśśrī nēmayē yēna haritalpāhi bhōgavat
śrībhujaṅgī mahābhōgō na tr̥ṇāyāpyamanyata // Ādi.16.32 [anuṣṭubh]

namaḥ pārśvāya sāmrājyamēkacchatrē jagattrayē
yasyākhyātīva dharaṇastridhr̥tātapavāraṇaṁ // Ādi.16.33 [anuṣṭubh]

namastrailōkyadurvāramāravīramadacchidē
mahāvīrāya bhūpēndrastūyamāna jayaśriyē // Ādi.16.34 [anuṣṭubh]

sa vahati kavitāguṇārṇavākhyāṁ
nanu bhuvanatritayēpyananyarūḍhāṁ
viṣayamavatarēdyadīya vācāṁ
caturadhikā jinaviṁśatiśśubhāya // Ādi.16.35 [puṣpitāgraṁ]


[p. 342]
nayavinayadhiyaḥ samantabhadrāḥ
vidadhatu vāṅmayadāma pūjyapādāḥ
nama iti paramākṣaradvayaṁ tē
mama japataḥ padamakṣaraṁ jinēndrāḥ // Ādi.16.36 [puṣpitāgraṁ]

end’ anēkastavanaṅgaḷiṁ stutiyisi tadanantarasamayadoḷ,

bharataṁ kāyōtsargado
ḷire cittanirōdhadiṁ saḍildoḍe tanu bhā
suraratnābharaṇaṅgaḷ
śarīradindudirduvamaratarukusumadavol // Ādi.16.37 [kandaṁ]

mattaṁ sākētanagaramaṁ baḷasida kanakaprākārada bāgilvāḍaṅgaḷoḷaṁ
rājamandirada gōpuradvāraṅgaḷoḷaṁ tanna purada pōpa barpa rājamārgadoḷaṁ
caturviṁśadarhatpratimāvirājamānahēmadāmavilambitamaṇighaṇṭāsamanvita-
vandanamālegaḷaṁ

puge poṟamaḍe tanna manaṁ
buguvantire tanna makuṭaśikharamanavu ne
ṭṭage tāguvantumāgire
jagadadhipanudāttabhaktiyiṁ māḍisidaṁ // Ādi.16.38 [kandaṁ]

tanage bharatēśvaraṁ vaṁ
danārthadiṁ sameda māle bharatadoḷadu vaṁ
danamāley emba pesaraṁ
tanage pesar‍māḍi kūḍe sandapudinnuṁ // Ādi.16.39 [kandaṁ]

priyadharmanr̥patiyaṁ nō
ḍi yathā rājā tathā prajā embavolō
jeyoḷōjegoṇḍu dharma
priyarādar prajegaḷuṁ samastāvaniyoḷ // Ādi.16.40 [kandaṁ]

matt’ itta vr̥ṣabhanāthanuṁ vr̥ṣabhasēna kumbha dr̥ḍharatha śatrudamana dēvaśarma
yaśōbāhu dēvāgni agnidēva āgnigupta citragupta mitrāgni haḷadhara mahīdhara
[p. 343]
mahēndra vasudēva vasundharācaḷa mērudhara mērubhūti sarvayaśa sar‍vayajña
sarvagupta sar‍vapriya sar‍vadēva sar‍vavijaya vijayagupta vijayamitra vijaya aparājita
vasumitra viśvasēna sādhuṣēṇa satyadēva dēvasatya satyagupta satyamitra śarmiḷa
vinīta saṁ[va]ra munigupta munidatta muniyajña munidēva guptayajña mitrayajña
svayambhu bhagadēva bhagadatta bhagaphalgu, mitraphalgu, prajāpati, sarvasaṅgha, varuṇa,
dhanapāla, maghava, tējōrāśi mahāvīra mahāratha [viśālākṣa] mahā[bala]
suviśāla vajra vajra [sāra] candracū[ḍa] mēghēśvara mahāsvara kaccha mahākaccha
namivinami baḷa atibaḷa vajrabaḷa baḷārāti bhadrabaḷa nandabaḷa mahābhō[ga]
nandimitra kāmadēva anupamarembeṇbattu nālvar gaṇadharadēvaruṁ, nālsāsiṟa-
dēḻnūṟayvadimbar sakaḷapūrvadhararuṁ, nālsāsiradainūṟayvadimbar śikṣakaruṁ
ombaisāsirvaravadhijñānigaḷuṁ irpattusāsirvarkēvaḷajñānigaḷuṁ irpattu
sāsiradaṟunūrvar vikriyardhiprāptaruṁ pannirchāsiradēḻnūrayvadimbar
manaḥpar‍yayajñānigaḷuṁ anibare vādigaḷuṁ modalāge eṇbattunālsāsiradeṇbatta
nālvar munipatigaḷuṁ mūṟalakkeyumayvattusāsira brahmimukhyāryikāgaṇamuṁ
mūṟulakke dr̥ḍhabratādiśrāvakaruṁ aydulakke suvrate modalāge paramaśrāvakiyaruṁ
aydulakke bhavanāmarādicaturvidhadēvanikāyamuṁ pakṣicatuṣpadasarīsr̥pāditir‍ya-
gjātigaḷuṁ berasu dhar‍māmr̥tavarṣadiṁ dharmakṣētraṅgaḷoḷ bhavyasasyaṅgaḷananēkabrata-
phalavinataṅgaḷ māḍi caturuttarāśītilakṣapubbaṅgaḷoḷage padinālkudivasadāyuṣya-
muṇṭ ene kaiḷāsaparvatada siddhakūṭadoḷ pauṣyamāsada paurṇamī dinadandu
yōgapalyaṅkāsanadindaṁ yōganirōdhadoḷ pūrvābhimukhanāgirdaṁ;
annegamittal,

bharataṁ darśanadoḷ maṁ
daramā prāgbhārabhūtaḷambaregaṁ nī
ḷdire kaṇḍu vismitāntaḥ
karaṇanadarkagidu nāḍeyuṁ cintisidaṁ // Ādi.16.41 [kandaṁ]

divadiniḻidōṣadhidruma
mavanītaḷamanujamaraṇajanmajarāsaṁ
bhavabhayamaṁ kiḍisi diva
kkavayavadindaḍare nōḍidaṁ yuvarājaṁ // Ādi.16.42 [kandaṁ]


[p. 344]
narasamitige bēḍidudaṁ
nirantaraṁ koṭṭu kalpavr̥kṣaṁ pōgal
suralōkakkudyatamā
gire kaṇḍaṁ svapnasamayadoḷ gr̥hapatiyuṁ // Ādi.16.43 [kandaṁ]

vararatnadvīpaṁ bhā
suraratnāḷiyananārataṁ koṭṭu vasuṁ
dharegabhradatta negeya
lkire kaṇḍaṁ bharatamantrimukhyanumāgaḷ // Ādi.16.44 [kandaṁ]

nelasirda vajrapañjara
malaṟuvinaṁ pāyda sindhurārātiyanu
jjvalatanuvanabhrapathada
tta laṅghisalkirdudaṁ camūpati kaṇḍaṁ // Ādi.16.45 [kandaṁ]

mattaṁ jayapriyatanūjaṁ

tārānikarāvēṣṭita
tārāpati[yā] samastasuralōkamumaṁ
nērittu beḷagi pōpuda
nā rātriyoḷintanantavīr‍yaṁ kaṇḍaṁ // Ādi.16.46 [kandaṁ]

surarājamanaḥpriye śaci
verasu yaśasvatiyumā sunandeyumāgaḷ
piriduṁ śōkadoḷire yuva
tiratnamenisida subhadre kanasaṁ kaṇḍaḷ // Ādi.16.47 [kandaṁ]

mattaṁ vārāṇasīnagarādhīśvaranakampanatanayaṁ,

dharaṇītaḷaghanatamamaṁ
karagisi bhāsvatkaraṅgaḷiṁ gaganataḷa
kkiradaḍarva visphuraddina

vyasanavyucchittiyoḷ dhār‍mikajanajanitānandasandōhavidyā
rasadoḷ saṁsārasārōdayaviracitadoḷ vāgvadhūmudreyoḷ mu
drisi nindattāditīrthēśvarana caritadoḷ vākyamāṇikyakōśaṁ // Ādi.16.80 [mahāsragdhare]

bhāsuradēvakōṭivibhuvappamaharddhikan appa vāsavaṁ
gāsanakampamaṁ paḍedu tīrthakaratvamanittanaśvarā
vāsamaneydisalkiduve ṣōḍaśabhāvaneyinde ṣōḍaśā
śvāsamaneyde bhāvisuge bhavyaranantasukhābhilāṣigaḷ // Ādi.16.81 [utpalamālike]


idu dēvēndramunīndravandyaparamajinēndramukhacandra
vākcandrikāprasaraprasādōdīrṇasūktikallōlamālākīrṇa
kavitāguṇārṇavapraṇītamappādipurāṇadoḷ
